Amidst Tense Mediterranean Situation, The Pope Tries Hard To Stop Italy From Joining The War. The Pope Met With The Italian Crown Prince Yesterday To Discuss The General Situation. The British Ambassador To Italy Has Departed To Return To His Post. Balkan Governments Have Exchanged Opinions For Days.

Vatican. The Italian Crown Prince and his Princess saw the Pope today, and they talked for thirty-five minutes. Then they went to see Vatican State Secretary Archbishop Maglione, and talked for a moment. After that, they went to St. Peter's Basilica to pray. When they left the Basilica, the crowds gathered outside cheered enthusiastically. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Rome. While Italian newspapers and radio stations were fiercely attacking Britain and France, the Pope of Rome made great efforts to fight against this war mood. In order to prevent Italy from joining the war, the Pope of Rome met yesterday with Italian Prince Umberto and Princess Marie-José, to discuss it, and said that Italy should remain neutral. (6th Universal News Agency Dispatch)

Rome. According to reliable sources from the Vatican today, Pope Pius believes that Italy's recent entry into the war is beyond doubt. It is reported that the Pope is deeply pessimistic about Italy's future policy and its possible consequences. Yesterday, a priest who heard the Pope speak in the Nive Church said that the Pope was in tears when he prayed to God "to protect Italy from the ravages of war." (6th United Press Dispatch)

London. British Ambassador to Italy Sir Roland is scheduled to return to Rome today to resume diplomatic talks. Diplomatic sources here recently stated that the recent attacks on Britain and France by Italian newspapers have intensified, so the mission of Ambassador Roland's trip is very difficult. It is reported that Italian Foreign Minister Ciano met with Counselor Charles of the British Embassy in Italy a few days ago and expressed surprise at the preventive measures taken by Britain in the Mediterranean, and said that Italy's attitude remained the same, and Britain did not need to take these measures. Later, Britain and France took other preventive measures, especially sending a fleet to Alexandria, Egypt. The Italian diplomatic authorities re-submitted their inquiries to Britain, asking for the truth, but Britain and France decided not to change their policies before the tone of Italian newspapers and the so-called "people's" demonstrations were improved. Observers believe that Italy's actions are two-pronged: on the one hand, providing guarantees to appease people's hearts, and on the other hand, adding threats to the negotiating countries. For this reason, although the government has provided guarantees to Yugoslavia that it will not infringe on its territory, the Yugoslav government and Britain and France still expressed doubts. In short, although the current crisis is not imminent, it is necessary to take the maximum preventive measures. Even if this crisis cannot be eliminated in one fell swoop, it can at least delay its onset. In addition, the general public is satisfied with Turkey's adherence to the mutual assistance agreement between Britain, France, and Turkey, believing that Turkey is worthy of being the mainstay of Southeast Europe. (6th Havas Dispatch)

London. According to news from Ankara, the governments of the Balkan countries are exchanging views in order to reach a consensus in their attitudes when dealing with any emergency. The precedent of the Scandinavian countries has taught the Balkan people a lesson, so the future of this matter is promising. It is said that the only hope for saving these countries lies in uniting before the crisis arrives. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Berlin. A senior German official said yesterday that Italy has been forced to approach Germany, and that Britain will be "forced to surrender to Germany" within eight months. (6th United Press Dispatch)

London. There is no confirmed news here about the Italian government's formal questions to Britain regarding the increased strength of the British fleet in the Mediterranean. It is heard that the British government's policy is to maintain and improve relations with Italy. As for the vigilance in the Mediterranean, it is due to the tone of some Italian newspapers and the public statements of well-known Italian figures. However, the British government continues to hope that British-Italian relations will improve and that peace in the Mediterranean region will be maintained. British Ambassador to Italy Sir Roland has now left for his post and is expected to arrive in Rome tonight. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Istanbul, Turkey. The Turkish pro-government newspaper "Tan Newspaper" declared today that if the war spreads to the Balkans, Turkey will immediately assist Britain and France. This is the reason for the special attention here to the development of the situation. (6th United Press Dispatch)

Bulgarian Defense Minister Declares Neutrality

Sofia. Defense Minister General Daskalov made a speech at the World War Veterans Memorial Meeting, solemnly declaring Bulgaria's determination to avoid getting involved in the vortex of war. His speech roughly said that Bulgaria is willing to maintain a neutral position at all times, and the Bulgarian people are willing to sacrifice everything to defend the country's independence and peace. (6th Huitong Dispatch)

German-Southern Economic Standing Committee to Begin Work This Morning

Capital of Yugoslavia. The German-Southern Economic Standing Committee is scheduled to begin work tomorrow morning. According to the official announcement, there are two issues that the committee should discuss: (1) determining the import quota of goods between the two countries; (2) determining the trade system between Southern countries and the German protectorate provinces of Bohemia and Moravia. The German delegation has a total of six representatives, with Landefliet, an advisor to the country's Ministry of Economy, as the chief representative. The Southern delegation has a total of nine representatives, with Biriya, the deputy minister of the Ministry of Economy, as the chief representative. (6th Havas Dispatch)

Many British Warships Arrive in Greek Waters. Double Tracks Laid on Egyptian Railways. British Nationals in Hungary Ordered to Evacuate.

Capital of Switzerland. According to news from Berlin, Britain has sent many technicians to the capital of Turkey, and many British warships have arrived in Greek waters. In addition, Britain has also inquired with the authorities of Bulgaria whether the Allied forces of Britain and France can be allowed to pass through the country if necessary. As for the British nationals in Hungary, they have all been ordered to evacuate. The German authorities were quite disturbed after hearing the news and are now watching the situation closely, and will never allow Britain and France to take the initiative. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Port of Constanta, Romania. The local authorities have recently taken some safety measures. Any ship that wants to enter this port must explain the reason and submit a report on the crew and the goods carried. In addition, all foreigners are prohibited from entering the port's docks. Several British people were arrested because their reasons for living in the country were insufficient. The British Consulate will protest to the authorities in Rome about this matter. (5th Havas News Agency Dispatch)

Cairo, Egypt. The situation in the Mediterranean is more tense than before, and the Suez Port is strategically more important, so it is necessary to strengthen its defense. The government authorities have appointed many experts to study it, and it is heard that they have drafted a plan to lay double tracks on the railway from this city to the Suez Port. (6th Havas Dispatch)

Sofia. Regarding the news that Turkey is concentrating troops on the border with Greece, the semi-official Bulgarian News Agency issued a statement authorized by the official, stating that the Bulgarian government has not received this news, so all kinds of speculation are unfounded. (6th Havas Dispatch)

Istanbul, Turkey. News from the capital of Bulgaria said that Turkey has massed a large number of troops on the Greek border, and it is said that this matter is related to the activities of the British navy in the eastern Mediterranean, and is the result of Britain's instigation. The semi-official Anatolian News Agency here was authorized by the official to clearly deny this, and said that those who enlisted in the reserve army for training were dismissed on schedule after the training was completed, and there was no delay. (6th Havas Dispatch)

Istanbul, Turkey. The "Yeni Sabah Newspaper" here recently published a report that it is rumored that 50,000 Italian troops are now concentrated on the Italian-owned Dodecanese Islands in the Mediterranean, ready to land on the Turkish coast at any time. This statement is purely fabricated, and its purpose is to create a tense situation in the Mediterranean. The strength of the Italian navy is not enough to control the eastern Mediterranean. If an expeditionary force is sent to attack Turkey, the food and ammunition it needs will be difficult to obtain a steady supply. This situation is also known in Italy. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Italian Students Demonstrate, Shouting Anti-British and Anti-French Slogans

Rome. About 100 students in Milan held an organized anti-Allied demonstration on the weekend. It is learned that this group of young students marched in columns through the streets, shouting "Long live Germany" and "Death to Britain and France," and used chalk to draw on the walls "We want Hitler to London, Mussolini to Paris." (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Italian Minister of Transportation Leaves Hungary for Home

Budapest. Italian Minister of Transportation Fantuli came here to inquire and has been here for several days. He left for home tonight. Before leaving, he made a speech, saying that the friendship between Italy and Hungary has always been close, and this trip has provided more proof. (5th Havas Dispatch)

South Africa Prepares to Deploy Troops to Defend East Africa

New York. Passengers on the "New York City" mail ship arrived here from the Cape of Good Hope. It is said that the South African authorities are preparing to send troops to defend British East Africa when Italy joins the war. It is also said that the world's second largest mail ship, the "Queen Mary," was seen moored off the Cape of Good Hope in mid-April, but it sailed away immediately. (6th United Press Dispatch)

British Ambassador to Turkey Visits Bulgarian Government, Rumored to Make Three Suggestions

Sofia. British Ambassador to Turkey Sir Hughe Knatchbull-Hugessen is visiting here. Yesterday, he and the country's Minister to Bulgaria, Ryle, went to the suburbs for a tour. The content of the talks between Sir Hughe Knatchbull-Hugessen and King Boris the day before is being kept secret here. It is heard that Sir Hughe Knatchbull-Hugessen will formally visit the Bulgarian government today after attending the military parade of Bulgaria's Bravery Day. (6th Huitong News Agency Dispatch)

Istanbul, Turkey. The Turkish Republican Newspaper carried this morning that Sir Hughe Knatchbull-Hugessen made three suggestions to the Bulgarian government on behalf of the British government, as the price for Bulgaria to participate in the Balkan anti-German united front: (1) Expand trade between Britain and Bulgaria; (2) Britain grants Bulgaria credit loans; (3) Britain will come forward to mediate in order to resolve the various disputes between Bulgaria and its neighbors. After the last World War, Bulgaria was forced to sign the Treaty of Neuilly, losing a lot of territory, while neighboring countries expanded a lot of land. In contrast, Bulgaria repeatedly complained, using the slogan of restoring lost territory. Britain knows this, so British Ambassador to Turkey Knatchbull-Hugessen informed the Bulgarian government of Britain's suggestions and stated that the Turkish government is also prepared to assist Bulgaria. (6th Huitong Dispatch)

British Public Opinion Demands Improvement of Government Institutions. There Will Be a Great Debate in the House of Commons Today.

London. The attention of the local newspapers is still focused on the future debate in Parliament on the Norwegian war. Some commentators believe that before the government has the opportunity to explain its handling and answer many complex questions, it should not draw conclusions for the time being. The Times expresses its deep admiration for Prime Minister Chamberlain's energy and courage, but said that in terms of personnel, certain improvements should be made. In the wartime cabinet, greater concentration and driving force are needed, and more time is needed for forward-looking thinking. The newspaper also said that the concept that the wartime cabinet is completely separated from the views of various officials is no longer supported by most people. The most important figures in the cabinet should each have their own representatives, such as the recent example of the chiefs of staff of the three services (Army, Navy, and Air Force) each having a representative. These representatives can slightly reduce the pressure on the work of some cabinet members. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

London. A Reuters reporter stationed in the Parliament lounge claimed that no one is prepared to predict what will happen in tomorrow's House of Commons debate. The situation of the debate depends on the content of Prime Minister Chamberlain's speech and its impact on the entire House. It is expected that the three ministers of the Army, Navy, and Air Force will all speak. The natural way would be for either Army Secretary Stanley or Air Secretary Hoare to end the debate on Tuesday, and for Navy Secretary Churchill to end the debate on Wednesday. However, if a severe attack is triggered tomorrow, Churchill may come forward to intervene on the first day. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

London. The "Daily Mail" here recently published in a prominent position a letter from a certain anonymous but well-known member of the House of Commons. The letter also lists a hypothetical list of cabinet members. The list includes Lloyd George, who served as Prime Minister during the previous European War, and all major positions are given to Labor Party members. The list has Halifax as Prime Minister, Churchill, Lloyd George, and Eden as ministers without portfolio, Morrison as Chancellor of the Exchequer, Attlee as Foreign Secretary, Sinclair as Navy Secretary, Hudson as Air Secretary, Moore-Brabazon as Army Secretary, and Woolton as Minister of Economic Warfare. Well-informed sources believe that at the time of the British army's withdrawal from Norway, it is extremely important for the prestigious Lloyd George to take the stage. Even the conservative newspaper "The Times," which usually criticizes the Labor Party, also believes that this kind of important government reorganization plan that can consolidate the entire foundation of the government and represent the entire strength of the country has already become the general public's psychology in the past few days. (6th United Press Dispatch)

United States Closely Watching British Political Situation, Fearing Japan Will Take the Opportunity to Invade the Dutch East Indies

Washington. People here are paying close attention to the British political situation after the Allied forces withdrew from southern Norway. According to the opinions of political commentators, recent developments have caused genuine anxiety among important officials in Washington. Some parties are deeply afraid that another setback for the Allied countries will prompt Japan to take action against the Dutch East Indies, and the United States will also be involved. It is heard that officials here are quite worried about this possibility. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Washington. President Roosevelt is now resting at his private residence in Hyde Park City, New York. Because he has not received a telegram from the State Department urging him to do so, he will probably continue to rest for a few days before returning to Beijing. (6th Havas Dispatch)

New York. The New York Tribune published an article saying that the democratic countries can get some comfort from the situation caused by the Allied defeat in Norway, that is, this move has deeply shaken the hearts of the British people. Those who made them encounter this were the experienced and prudent heads of state. Whether they will allow these people to leave the government can be seen in a few days. However, they at least know now that what they are doing is a real war, and all wars cannot be won by waiting quietly. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Dissatisfaction in Canada over British War Actions

New York. The New York Times carried a report from Ottawa, saying that some of Canada's dissatisfaction with the British government's war actions is now becoming more and more obvious. The report also said that here it is believed that the failure of the British army in Norway, for the two places of Wye Andalsnes and Namsos, the dissatisfaction has increased. Many people feel that this not only shows Britain's failure, but also reflects Canada's own war efforts. Many non-official Canadians are too worried and uneasy about Britain's failure, so they complain. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Distribution of Food in Britain

London. Food Minister Lord Woolton announced today that, in view of the suspension of supplies from Denmark, the public must prepare for the possibility that the per capita ration of butter will soon be reduced to the previous amount. If he cannot be completely sure of the sufficient supply of sugar in the second half of this year, the per capita ration will also be reduced. He intends that the convenience of cold storage may not be enough to cope with the worst possible situation that may come. We have started the construction of cold storage warehouses in eight places far apart in the country. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

British Navy Secretary Churchill Expands His Power

London. The "Daily Telegraph" and "News Chronicle" have recently reported that Navy Secretary Churchill has now obtained greater power to adjust and implement the government's various decisions on combat. The "Daily Telegraph" also explained that, henceforth, various decisions related to the Army, Navy, and Air Force will still be made by the respective staff departments, but all issues that must be decided by the government will be submitted to the government by Navy Secretary Churchill in his capacity as Chairman of the Cabinet Defense Committee, and implemented after approval. This reform was caused by criticism from all sides that the government had failed to implement decisions quickly after making them. Prime Minister Chamberlain will present a report on the expansion of Navy Secretary Churchill's power when the House of Commons holds a debate within a few days. (6th Havas Dispatch)

Britain Has Not Yet Rejected Soviet Suggestions

London. It is heard that the Soviet Union's trade proposals are currently being considered by various departments of the British government. It is untrue to say that they have been rejected. It is heard that the British side has not made any decision on this matter. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Soviet-German Summer Flights Begin

Moscow. The Moscow-Berlin airline began its summer flights yesterday. (5th TASS News Agency Dispatch)

Yugoslavia Rejects German Tourists

London. The British Broadcasting Corporation's radio station recently broadcast a message saying that Germany had asked the authorities of Yugoslavia to allow thousands of German tourists to travel to the country this summer, but the Yugoslav authorities refused, but said that German women and children can enter the Southern countries at will. (6th Havas Dispatch)

Lower Danube River Flooded

Bucharest. The Black Sea is stormy, and many ships are unable to reach Constanta because of the wind. The lower reaches of the Danube River and its estuary have been flooded. Two dikes near Galati have collapsed. The low-lying areas of the city of Galati have become a swamp. Several warehouses have been submerged in the water, and several trains with timber inside have been washed away by the water. (6th Huitong Dispatch)

Belgian Prime Minister Reaffirms Neutrality Resolution

Brussels. Belgian Prime Minister Pierlot made a speech in Charleroi, reaffirming Belgium's determination to maintain neutrality and independence, saying that Belgium is no longer a battlefield for others to resolve their disputes. Belgian territory has heavy defenses, and the troops guarding the territory are all prepared to defend the country to the best of their ability. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Soviet-Swedish Trade Increases Greatly

Capital of Sweden. According to news received here, trade between Sweden and Soviet Russia will increase greatly recently, because the two countries will start formal business negotiations in the near future. (6th Huitong Dispatch)

Rivers Rise Sharply in Iraq

Capital of Iraq. The Euphrates River has risen sharply, and several embankments have collapsed. Thousands of acres of farmland have become swamps. Traffic between here and Damascus in the Syrian Republic has also been interrupted. The authorities have taken various measures to prevent the expansion of the flood. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Page 6

Anglo-French-Norwegian Allied Forces Encircle Narvik, German Planes Aid in Northern Norway with Over a Hundred Sorties, British Admiralty Announces Destroyer Sunk

Berlin: Today's German military communique stated that the enemy has transported more artillery pieces from the north, but there were no major military operations in the Narvik area yesterday. German military aircraft were active near Narvik, dropping a heavy bomb that hit an enemy warship, and also bombed enemy camps and ammunition depots. One ammunition depot was hit and exploded. German troops advanced northward from Grong, south-southeast of Namsos. Central and southern Norway are now quiet. The fortress built on Mount Hegra has been captured by German forces. Two British airships were attacked and damaged by German military aircraft near the northern coast of Norway. A British submarine was captured by German forces in the Kattegat Strait. The captain of the submarine was arrested. It was found that the submarine was severely damaged by a mine. Subsequently, a German patrol boat towed it into the harbor. In the area of Terschelling, German forces shot down two British Bristol Blenheim military aircraft. There were no particularly important events on the Western Front. (Reuter telegram, 6th)

London: A Reuters military correspondent stated that the Allied forces are now carrying out a well-planned offensive against Narvik. Before carrying out the bombardment, the Allied forces warned civilians. Although this is tantamount to notifying the German forces of the Allied forces' intentions, after the evacuation of the residents in the city is completed, the Allied naval commander will have a wider scope of operations. The German forces have built a continuous series of concrete machine-gun nests, which must be cleared one by one, so the progress is quite slow. The outskirts are not suitable for armored vehicles. German bombers will not be able to gain an advantage. The situation is similar to Trondheim, because the Allied anti-aircraft guns are already in place, and the German air bases are relatively far away. (Reuters telegram, 6th)

Stockholm: German forces are now trying to gain air superiority in the Narvik area. It is reported that no fewer than one hundred German planes flew north in one day. News of isolated resistance in central Norway continues to arrive. However, the only organized Norwegian army is said to be the division commanded by General Fleischer in the Narvik area, totaling 25,000 men. Except for a portion of 2,000 men who have been transferred to the Trondheim area to fight, the rest are said to be intact. It is reported that the Norwegian army has entered the Gratangen Valley and eliminated 1,000 German soldiers. According to news from Oslo, German forces have captured 10,000 Norwegians and are said to be using them for agricultural and industrial work in Norway. London estimates that the German forces besieged in Narvik number between 3,000 and 4,000. According to official sources, military operations in that area are still ongoing, but the adverse weather makes it difficult to predict a swift result. (Reuters telegram, 6th)

London: The War Office recently released a communique stating, "The war in the Narvik port area in northern Norway is still ongoing. There has been no major development except for some activity by the enemy air force." (Havas telegram, 5th)

London: The British Broadcasting Corporation radio station recently broadcast news stating that the German forces have repeatedly launched attacks north of Narvik port in Norway, but were all repelled by the Allied forces. The port has been completely surrounded by the Allied forces. As for the area east of the Austerda River, the war is still ongoing. According to news from Sweden, Norwegian troops have repelled 3,000 German soldiers in the Rofotnas area. The town of Aas is still burning after being bombed by German planes. The enemy believes that King Haakon VII of Norway is now in Kirkenes and has flown to that area for heavy bombardment. (Havas telegram, 6th)

London: A correspondent for the Daily Express stationed in Stockholm recently telegraphed that the troops concentrated by Germany in the port of Memel and along the Baltic coast have already been transferred to the southeast of the country. (Havas telegram, 6th)

Stockholm: According to reliable sources, one hundred German planes flew to Narvik port in northern Norway this morning. American Educator Arrives in Shanghai, Speaks of China's Resistance to the End, The Stage of Japanese Negotiations Has Passed, Morale in the Interior is High and Belief is Firm

According to reports, a certain internationally renowned American educator recently arrived in Shanghai after touring various provinces in western China. He stated that the stage for Japan to negotiate peace with China has now passed. Chairman Chiang has formulated a plan to promote China's heavy industry, which within three years will enable China to independently produce all military equipment needed for the war of resistance. "The people within Free China are all optimistic and confident, and fully support the government's war policy." This educator has met with dozens of important figures including Chairman Chiang, H.H. Kung, T.V. Soong, Neng Yun, Dr. Jing Hwai-lin, Deputy Minister of Propaganda Dong Xian-guang, and leaders of the Communist Party.

Resist to the End, No Compromise

When interviewing Chairman Chiang, he inquired about the possibility of China manufacturing its own airplanes and cannons. Chairman Chiang replied that the Chinese government will implement this plan according to a set procedure. Furthermore, according to senior officials, Japan had asked a confidant of Chairman Chiang to convey a message, attempting to contact Chairman Chiang for negotiations. Chairman Chiang ignored the Japanese proposal. The Japanese attempt has failed. Government officials frankly admit that China has suffered significant losses as a result of the war. However, there is currently a common view among the Chinese government and the public, which can be summarized as "No compromise with the enemy, resolutely carry out resistance to the end, to seek national rejuvenation."

Economic Institutions Becoming More Stable. Government officials admit that China's final victory depends on four key elements: (1) money, (2) military supplies, (3) manpower, and (4) automobile transportation. The most serious of these is the issue of money, which encompasses the entire national economic organization. However, officials firmly believe that the economic situation in "Free China" can be readjusted through control measures. The large-scale relocation of factories and people to southwestern China has caused drastic changes in social institutions, presenting the government with many difficulties. However, the situation is now gradually improving, and given time, economic and social order can be restored, and the overall situation will become more stable.

Training Elite Troops Facilitates Transportation. There is absolutely no problem with manpower. There are currently four million well-trained soldiers, and new recruits are being trained every month. Regarding the issue of automobile transportation, there are large fleets of trucks in the north, but most drivers lack sufficient mechanical knowledge, resulting in negligence. Under the effective management of Minister of Communications Chang Chia-ao, the number of trucks has increased sharply. Chang stated that the main problem lies in training a large number of truck drivers with mechanical knowledge, who know how to repair and properly maintain the vehicles to prevent unnecessary waste. Regarding this point, Chang has ordered the establishment of repair workshops along important highways.

Chairman Chiang is the Supreme Leader

The American educator went on to say that regarding the political situation in "Free China," rumors of friction between the Kuomintang and the Communist Party should be refuted. According to reports, such rumors are often heard by Chinese people outside "Free China," but they are completely unfounded. He had frank discussions with responsible leaders of the Kuomintang and the Communist Party, and knew that no one understood their common mission of defeating and driving out the enemy better than them. They are cooperating sincerely and striving together in various ways to accomplish this mission. Chairman Chiang has rapidly risen to the position of supreme leader of the country. He believes that Chairman Chiang, due to his position in the government, has placed himself above party or factional views, and has become the "cement" that unites the Kuomintang and the Communist Party.

National Morale and Military Morale are Equally High

It is heard that the number of military supplies provided by the Soviet Union to China is very large, but the official information on the exact amount is not available. In his opinion, as the war continues, military medical care will become a serious problem. Private hospitals and independent medical teams have done their best to remedy the alarming situation caused by the shortage of medicines. The Red Cross is now formulating a plan to provide effective medical services at the lowest cost. What is more important than all the wartime activities in "Free China" is that everyone has the spirit of enduring hardship and seeking a bright future. National morale and military morale are equally high, because they embrace belief and optimism and do not hesitate to sacrifice. There is absolutely no talk of peace in "Free China" today. Everyone is united, carrying out the war as completely as possible. The war may last for several years, but he firmly believes that the Chinese government and people, under the leadership of Chairman Chiang, will not end the war of resistance until China has completely gained independence and freedom.

Run on Deposits Subsides, Financial Stability Increases, Foreign Exchange Stabilizes after Support, Ministry of Finance Plans Measures to Crack Down on Speculation

Reuters, Hong Kong, 6th. A leading Chinese banking figure told a Reuters reporter today that although the authorities withdrew support for the legal tender foreign exchange control in the Shanghai exchange market on Thursday, there is no reason to doubt the legal tender. This doubt comes from the activities of speculators, whose irresponsible actions will be condemned by the world. The Chinese authorities intend to continue to support the legal tender, and the recent withdrawal of support is only temporary. The existing silver reserves available to the stabilization fund have increased slightly, so the authorities are confident that they can handle the exchange situation.

Since the Chinese government declared its determination to maintain the monetary system and stabilize foreign exchange, and the bankers' and money changers' guilds truthfully denied restricting withdrawals, the market stabilized slightly yesterday, and people's hearts gradually calmed down. However, rumors have not completely subsided. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency specifically interviewed the secretary of the Bankers' Association and a member of the Money Changers' Association yesterday. According to them, the member banks and firms have been preparing everything since rumors spread in the market that withdrawals would be restricted again. Although the current environment is difficult, fortunately the strength of the banking and money changing industries is sufficient, so they can cope with it easily. The rumor that the banking and money changing industries held an emergency meeting on Sunday is false. It is hoped that all circles will not easily believe rumors, so as not to fall into the conspiracy of villains.

Shanghai's Capital Still Needs to Be Dispersed

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency met with a leader in the banking industry yesterday. According to him, the order and safety of the Shanghai concessions can be maintained to a considerable extent, so refugees from all over the country regard Shanghai as a haven of peace during the war. For two and a half years, more and more people have gathered, and the capital has increased accordingly, so the capital in Shanghai is becoming more and more abundant. Although the theory of transferring capital to the southwest has been very popular in recent years, although many in the banking and money changing industries have implemented it, large-scale transfer may not be achievable in one step, so how to coordinate and take care of dispersing Shanghai's capital and make it run on the right track still requires further efforts. The financial community should set an example, so that finance can gradually get on the right track, so as not to fail the government's expectations.

The Financial Community Should Set an Example. He also said that Shanghai's economic prosperity is contrary to the wartime national policy. The financial community did not examine it carefully, but only took its own superficial interests as a prerequisite, and provided as much assistance as possible, or used other convenient methods, to promote the abnormal development of the economy in the occupied areas. As a result, it violated the proper strategy of the wartime national policy, and some in the financial community even bought and sold foreign exchange and gold, hoarding daily necessities, in order to make profits. This kind of situation is a violation of government prohibitions, so it is hoped that the financial community should remember the government's difficulty in supporting wartime finance and the century-old plan of national life, and have a sense of their due responsibility, and promptly stop engaging in improper business, so as not to encourage speculation and affect people's livelihood.

Foreign Exchange Loosens, Gold Still Rises

Previously, the Foreign Exchange Stabilization Fund Committee restricted the supply of foreign exchange on the Shanghai black market, causing the market exchange rate to shrink sharply, and speculators rushed in. Yesterday morning, the Hong Kong and Shanghai Banking Corporation announced its listed prices: British exchange was three pence one two five longer one two five, and US exchange was four yuan five jiao, longer one eight seven five. Legitimate needs of various industries have been supplied. At the same time, the market believes that the Hong Kong Foreign Exchange Stabilization Fund Committee has come out to maintain it, so the actual transaction market is higher than the HSBC listing price. However, the gold market rose against foreign exchange due to speculators' collection. The morning closing price was six thousand nine hundred and sixty-five yuan, and the afternoon closing price was seven thousand and ten yuan. The legal foreign exchange listing price of the Central Bank remains the same, without any change.

Withdrawals Subside, Finance Tends to Stabilize

Yesterday (Monday), after the banks and firms opened at 9:00 a.m., general depositors did not withdraw much money from the banks and firms because they confirmed that the rumors of restricting withdrawals were unreliable. At the same time, the financial market has stabilized due to the maintenance of the Foreign Exchange Stabilization Fund Committee and the interbank lending of the Central Bank, Bank of China, Agricultural Bank, and Bank of Communications, as well as the adjustment of the bankers' and money changers' guilds. It is also heard that the Ministry of Finance attaches great importance to the Shanghai black market foreign exchange and has jointly planned remedies with the Ministry of Economic Affairs. Those who speculate in foreign exchange and hoard daily necessities will be investigated and punished, and illegal trading in the gold black market will be strictly cracked down on in order to relieve people's difficulties and maintain security.

The Court is Ordered to Strictly Crack Down. It was also learned yesterday that since the drastic changes in the black market foreign exchange last week, the courts of the First Special Zone and the Second Special Zone of this port have received instructions from Chongqing, ordering them to strictly crack down on speculation, manipulation, and hoarding. Those who have obtained solid evidence may be sentenced to long-term imprisonment or at least five years of imprisonment by the court.

Soaring Prices, Drastic Reduction in Purchasing Power, The Apparent Prosperity of the Commercial Market is Exhausted

Shanghai's price threat is serious, and the apparent prosperity of the commercial market is increasingly exposed. According to a leader in the cloth industry yesterday, Shanghai's prices have reached an unprecedented peak, and people's livelihood is extremely difficult. The commercial market of various industries has also been deeply affected. Now, except for daily necessities such as rice, coal, and flour, which can be saved, the rest lack purchasing power. Taking cloth as an example, it is also a kind of daily necessity, but the selling price of cotton yarn has repeatedly risen sharply. Ordinary cloth has risen to the price of silk in the past. Citizens cannot afford three meals a day, so how can they have the surplus to add clothes? Therefore, the turnover of various industries has decreased significantly. The same is true for other department stores. If this continues, the commercial market will be depressed, and factories will reduce work, which is a major hidden worry for the future of industry and commerce. At this time when the authorities are about to implement additional donations, it is hoped that the municipal authorities will stand up and seek ways to save the situation, cultivate tax sources, and maintain the market.

The Attitude of the Authorities. According to reliable sources, the authorities of the two concessions will take considerable measures to curb the speculation and manipulation of merchants due to the soaring prices in recent days. The plans are (1) to establish a food production and marketing cooperative to handle production and sales, (2) to issue notices to inform citizens. According to the authorities of the French Concession Police Department, from April 15 to May 1, 23 out of 80 stores were found to be in violation of regulations and were fined 200 yuan.

Use of Law. Currently, the authorities of the French Concession are making every effort to place the market under their jurisdiction, so that citizens from all walks of life pay close attention to it, because the prices in the market are often lower than those in the stores, so if citizens can pay attention to this and criticize it closely, prices may fall accordingly. According to Mr. Ge Bo, Assistant Secretary of the Public Works Department, the restrictions on prices by the authorities of the two concessions in the past can be said to have failed, so it is believed that it is necessary to use the law. This means that it is necessary to legislate to restrict prices, if the black exchange continues to tighten.

Food Problem

The authorities of the two concessions are now paying the most attention to food and flour. According to investigations, there are still 780,000 bags of rice in stock in this city, which is enough to supply the citizens of this city for six months. The highest rice price set last winter was 40 yuan, but now the rice price has soared to 54 yuan. The Price Stabilization Committee of the Public Concession and the French Concession of this port has scheduled a joint meeting this week to discuss this matter. The rice industry believes that the main reasons for the failure of rice price limits in the past were the scarcity of sources and the restrictions imposed by the Japanese in the suburbs of Shanghai, so it is hoped that the establishment of a production and marketing cooperation mechanism can enable both parties to the transaction in this port to gather together and trade at the lowest prices under the supervision of the authorities of the concessions. However, this matter is still in the preparatory stage.

Selling Coal Balls at a Reduced Price

Since the black exchange in this city fluctuated a few days ago, coal ball merchants took the opportunity to raise market prices, and each load rose to nearly 10 yuan, which generally threatened civilians. Guohua and Dongfang Coal Ball Factories have now decided to hold a sale of coal balls at a reduced price from 1:00 p.m. to 3:00 p.m. every day, with the price set at 8 yuan and 5 jiao per load (100 city catties). However, for the sake of popularity, each household is limited to one load. The method is to pay for the goods first, and then pick them up the next day. There are no cartage fees, but telephone orders will not be accepted. The locations of the two factories' sales are listed below.

Guohua Factory Sales: 6 locations, 394 Route Tenant de la Tour, 625 Connaught Road, 195 Avenue du Roi Albert, 111 West Gate Road, 819 Sinza Road, 269 Seymour Road.

Dongfang Factory Sales: 10 locations, Dongfang Coal Ball Factory Branch, 29 Langbing Road, and 203 Muirhead Road, and Yuanyuan Coal Ball Company Service Station, 155 Route Tenant de la Tour, 114 Maichiqi Road, 13 Annan Road, 467 Avenue Road, 117 Jessfield Road, 151 Rue Bourgeat, 199 Chihli Road, Edward Avenue Edward Market.

The Coal and Firewood Association of this city is experiencing difficulties in its business due to the high wholesale price of coal balls, which is as high as 170 yuan. In order to maintain the business of the industry, it has held a district registration to investigate the actual situation of various industries, so as to request improvement of the business from the large coal companies. It is heard that the French Concession is divided into three districts, and the Public Concession is divided into four districts. Once the registration work is completed, a meeting will be convened to discuss various improvement issues.

Tea Exports Surge, Benefiting the National Treasury

At Times, the National Treasury Benefits.

Tea is a special product of China, and the annual exports are always in the tens of millions of yuan. After the outbreak of the War of Resistance, the National Government vigorously promoted special products and encouraged exports, with great success. In the first quarter of this year, the national tea exports totaled 164,270 quintals, with a value of 43,569,392 yuan. In terms of value, it is several times higher than the same period last year. Green tea accounts for the majority. Although important cities in Jiangsu and Zhejiang have been occupied, the vast tea-producing areas in the interior are still guarded by the National Army, so tea production has not been greatly affected. According to Ningbo Customs statistics, tea exports in March alone reached 48,000 quintals, with a value of 16 million yuan. From January to March, the total was 95,028 quintals, with a value of 30,138,895 yuan, accounting for three-quarters of the total national tea exports. They are all purchased by the government's trade agencies and transported to Hong Kong for resale to Europe, America, and the Soviet Union. Exports through customs such as Shanghai in the occupied areas are less than a quarter of the total, so the government's wartime finances are improving.

Under the Shadow of High Prices, Strive to Relieve the Poor, Various Charitable Groups Continue to Operate, Wealthy Merchants and Giants Should Donate and Assist

The Pi Han Suo (Shelter from the Cold) at Yan's Residence on Difeng Road in this city was established by the Joint Disaster Relief Association of charitable organizations last winter after borrowing vacant land from the Public Works Department of the Public Works Department. Since it began to take in poor people on the street on February 1 of this year, it has greatly benefited them. As of the end of April, it has taken in a total of 876 people. Now that the weather is turning warm, it was originally intended to end the operation, but in view of the fact that these people are the poorest citizens, once they are disbanded, they will still be reduced to the streets, which is closely related to social security. It has now been decided to abandon the name Pi Han Suo and reorganize it into a Vagrant Reformatory, hoping to give them time to reform them, provide education, and teach them production technology, so that they can become something in the future. The Shanghai Pharmaceutical Industry and Pharmaceutical Industry Association held a sale of plain rice at the Gion Dharma Assembly. Now that many poor people are buying it, it has increased to 7,000 catties per day. The plain rice sale at Moore Church and the porridge distribution at the Buddhist Association are also still ongoing. Since high prices make it difficult to stop the work of relieving the poor.

After the Increase in Public Bus Fares, Income Has Increased Compared to Before

The British Public Bus Company issued 35,000 yuan in substitute tokens and 160,000 yuan in substitute coins due to the lack of subsidiary currency in this city. Now that the panic of subsidiary currency has been resolved, the substitute currency has been gradually recovered. Two-thirds of the paper tokens have been recovered, and it is expected that it will not be difficult to recover them all within this month. As for the substitute coins, because they are easy to carry, they are mostly stored by passengers, so the recovery is still small. Since the bus fare increased in the middle of last month, the number of passengers has decreased by a quarter every day compared to the past, but due to the increase in price, although the number of passengers has decreased, the daily income has increased by more than 6,000 yuan, because in the past, the daily fare was about 220,000 yuan, but recently it has increased to more than 260,000 yuan. Regarding the resumption of driving in the northern district, the company authorities said that it is still impossible at present.

North China Mailing Parcels, Japanese and Puppet Also Implement Control

Dazhong News Agency said that since the North China Organization implemented foreign exchange settlement for exports last year, all luggage parcels and goods under 100 yuan are exempt from foreign exchange settlement. Recently, the control has been tightened, and the value of personal parcels sent from North China to Central China and South China must be approved by the "Joint Reserve Bank" before they can be transshipped.

After the New Exchange Transfer is Strengthened, There is No Need to Issue Exchange Transfer Certificates, and it is Feared that After the Issuance, the Public Will Hoard Them, so it Has Become a Prepared but Unused Item

Since the Bankers' and Money Changers' Guild implemented the new exchange transfer in July 28, strengthening the exchange transfer payment reserve, its preparation has been sufficient and has won the trust of various industries, and some foreign banks that refused to accept exchange transfers after August 13 have accepted them because of this. At that time, the banking and money changing industries had considered issuing exchange transfer certificates by the Bank United Preparation Committee in order to facilitate the daily acceptance of merchants due to the time limit of the bills. In addition to the fact that each firm could use the exchange transfer within its original limit, the Preparation Committee could pay the money of the drawer with the most connected industry exchange transfer bill with exchange transfer certificates. However, (1) since the industry preparation has been strengthened, it is expected that the exchange transfer certificate will be popular. If the general public trusts the exchange transfer certificate as much as they trust the legal tender, and they hoard them, the property deposited by various firms will be likely to be shelved, (2) at the beginning of the preparation of the exchange transfer certificate, rumors of circulating banknotes occurred on the market. Although the truth was clarified and the rumors stopped, it was appropriate to be cautious on the day when people were uneasy, so the exchange transfer certificate has not been used yet. Therefore, there is no need to issue it in the future.

Western Countries Work Together with China, Japan's Reaction to Closing the Door to China, Ahlers Criticizes Japan's Plundering Policy

English Greater Shanghai Evening Post said that English Greater Shanghai Evening Post financial editor Ahlers, with the support of the Chongqing Diplomatic Association, recently wrote a book entitled "Japan Closes the Open Door to China," published by Kelly & Walsh. The book details Japan's economic occupation in the occupied areas of China and Japan's plundering and exclusion of third countries, which are not allowed to engage in normal trade in China.

Presenting Definite Evidence

The first chapter of the book discusses "Why the West Should Care about China's Economy." The main idea is that after the end of the European War, China's great economic importance has attracted worldwide attention. Considering China's potential, China's past and current economic status is not enough. From 1937 to 1939, the foreign trade in western and southwestern China was extremely prosperous. If the Japanese had not imposed air raids and naval blockades, China's foreign trade volume would have been even larger. The second chapter discusses "The Meaning of the Open Door," saying that this kind of meaning is clear, practical and to the point.

However, the Japanese are determined to expand in China, and the economic system, policies, and objectives implemented in the occupied areas are the same everywhere, gradually excluding Westerners and oppressing the Chinese. The "Sino-Japanese Economic Cooperation" that the Japanese have been promoting for a long time is by no means mutually beneficial, but is entirely a one-sided "cooperation." It is only a pretext for the Japanese to plunder China's national and private property, in fact, forcing the Chinese to use their property to help the Japanese profit.

The remaining chapters of the book discuss China's shipping, railways, commerce, and trade, etc. One section states that Western countries are in the same boat, and even extreme friendly countries such as Germany and Italy have gained very little profit from their friendship with Japan.

Japanese Residents in Hongkou Formulate Punishment Rules

Illegitimate Profits Will Be Handled Appropriately

According to the Japanese Shanghai Mainichi Shimbun, the Japanese Consul General, Garrison, and Naval Special Marine Corps agreed on several punishment rules for Japanese residents at the Japanese Club on Pong Road last Saturday. Anyone who commits one of the following will be punished according to law: (1) Renting a house and subletting it to others in order to seek illegitimate profits, (2) Drinking excessively and making noise everywhere, (3) Suddenly acquiring illegitimate property in a short period of time, (4) Secretly selling opium, (5) Transporting various drugs to other ports.

Six American Ships to Sail the Far East

The Shanghai American Foreign Trade Shipping Company, a subsidiary of the United States Westward Shipping Company, officially announced yesterday that, starting from August 1939, the company has purchased ships from the United States Maritime Commission for voyages through the Strait of Georgia and the Far East. Six of these ships have been assigned specific schedules. Their routes will traverse the Pacific Ocean, traveling to and from the Far East. The names of the six ships are "Cape Cleare," "Cape Fairweather," "Cape Corinth," "Cape Meares," "Cape Sebastian," and "Cape Seppings." The ships' routes will start from the Strait of Georgia, passing through Japan, Shanghai, Hong Kong, and the Philippines. It is also learned that the first of the company's ships to arrive in Shanghai will be the "Cape Corinth," scheduled to sail from the Strait of Georgia on the 10th of this month. The company also hopes to increase the number of ships in the near future.

Carrying Gold and Silver to Shanghai Often Confiscated

It's Best to Transfer it to the Mainland, Don't Transport it to Shanghai to Support the Japanese

According to the Dazhong News Agency, when people carry gold and silver from the interior to Shanghai, they are often confiscated by the Japanese military along the way. On the 5th, a Mr. Zhou arrived in Shanghai from Changzhou by train. He claimed that Japanese military police in the train car inspected passengers for concealed gold and silver, checking everything from felt hats and collars to waistbands, sewn pockets, inner linings, socks, and shoe soles. Anything found was confiscated. It goes without saying that luggage, baskets, and crates were also routinely searched. Last month, a friend from northern Jiangsu Province who came to Shanghai also witnessed the strict search for gold and silver at the ports. If found, all would be confiscated, and any argument could lead to unexpected danger. The letter also included a few words: "Given the soaring gold prices and the Japanese facing financial difficulties, it is hoped that those who have gold and silver will find a way to transfer it to the interior and hand it over to the national bank for purchase. Do not violate national laws (as private transportation of gold and silver is prohibited by the government) by privately transporting it to Shanghai to support the Japanese, allowing them to exchange it for foreign currency to purchase military supplies to kill our people."

Nine American and British Ships, Six Japanese Ships

Recently, warships from various countries have gathered in the Huangpu River, their flags flying, creating a colorful scene. British Ships Traveling Between Europe and Asia Detour Around the Cape of Good Hope - The Mediterranean Situation Creates an Invisible Tension to Prevent Changes to the Suez Canal Navigation

Since the expansion of the European war and Italy's expression of its intentions, the Mediterranean situation has suddenly become tense. In addition to taking precautionary measures in the Mediterranean region, the British authorities have also instructed British ships that previously passed through the Suez Canal to detour around the Cape of Good Hope and enter the Indian Ocean. It has been learned that, although relations between Britain and Italy are unlikely to completely break down, all British ships sailing between Europe and Asia are now following the aforementioned instructions to prevent danger. The British ship "Shantung," which is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai from Scandinavia on the 13th of this month, will also detour around the Cape of Good Hope to sail to Shanghai.

French and Italian Ship Routes Remain Unchanged

France and Britain are allies, and tensions between Britain and Italy are bound to cause tensions between France and Italy. However, according to reliable sources, French ships sailing between Europe and Asia have not yet received detour orders from their home country, claiming that they have "taken certain measures" to adapt to changes in the situation at any time. It is also said that a French ship will depart from Shanghai via the Mediterranean Sea and return to its home country on the 8th of this month. As for Italian ships, they are still operating as usual, with no changes. The Conte Rosso mail ship, which is coming to China from Europe this time, has already passed Singapore and is in Hong Kong. It is expected to arrive in Shanghai around Thursday (the 9th) of this week and will return to Genoa from Shanghai on the 12th.

Female Boss of a Guiding Agency Kidnapped - A Dispute Over Recruiting Female Guides Leads to Kidnapping as Revenge - Now Held on Yuyuan Road

The Yong'an Guiding Agency is located in the rear厢房 on the upper floor of No. 11 Jingqingfang, Guangxi Road. It employs more than 20 female guides internally and is a small guiding agency. It was opened by Gu Xiujin, a middle-aged woman from Pudong (commonly called "Big Sister Gu," 39 years old), and has been in operation for more than half a year. Wang Yiqiu and Ni Adi are also employed as accountants and perform their respective duties. At around 12:30 PM yesterday, Gu Xiujin and Ni Adi were suddenly kidnapped, forced into a car, and sped off towards western Shanghai. They are now being held at a certain location on Yuyuan Road. Details of the situation have been learned and recorded below.

Sudden Appearance of Strange Men

At approximately 12:30 PM yesterday, while Gu and the accountant Ni Adi and the tea boy Zhang Maosheng (19 years old), etc., were having lunch at the agency, three strange men suddenly broke into the room. They immediately drew handguns and forbade anyone from making a sound. They then took out handcuffs and handcuffed Gu Xiujin and Ni Adi, both male and female, forcing them to go downstairs, walk out to the road at the entrance of the alley, and forced them into a waiting car with license plate number 17906, which turned south into North Sea Road and drove straight west. Afterwards, the agency reported the incident to the Laozha Police Station, which sent Chinese and Western detectives to investigate and inquire about the kidnapping.

No Payment Given

On the day before yesterday (the 4th), at approximately 7:00 PM, the agency received a phone call from a Mr. Wang in Room 4 of the Dahonglai Restaurant on Four Horses Road, requesting two female guides to serve drinks. The agency sent Wang Yaqing and Zhao Yuexian to respond to the request. After the drinking became less lively, they accompanied the guests to Room 404 of the Dadong Hotel at 9:00 PM, staying for about an hour, and then went to the Xindu Theater on Yu Qiaqing Road to watch a play. Soon after, they went together to Room 618 of the Jielu Hotel on Yu Qiaqing Road. A plan to indulge in lust was unsuccessful, causing dissatisfaction from the two guests. At dawn the next morning, at approximately 5:00 AM, they called the two female guides back to the agency, but they did not give them any payment. At that time, the time was calculated, Zhao Yuexian for eleven hours and Wang Yaqing for ten hours, and the cost of services should have been 21 yuan.

Outburst of Roaring

Wang and Zhao, the two women, suffered this blow, so they used the telephone to report to the agency. The agency owner Gu Xiujin, along with the accountant Ni Adi and Wang Yiqiu, rushed to reason with them. Unexpectedly, the two guests had already called seven or eight people from other places. When Gu and the others arrived, they quickly closed the three doors of the room and slapped Ni Adi several times. Fortunately, Wang Yiqiu was alert and took the opportunity to escape, calling two street patrol officers from 1803 and 1756. The two parties were brought to the police station. After a preliminary hearing by the police chief, it was ordered that 21 yuan be paid on the spot, and they were reprimanded before they left. At 2:00 PM, after a certain colleague came out to mediate, the other party insisted that Yong'an pay 30 yuan to settle the matter. As a result, because the conditions were harsh and difficult to comply with, unexpectedly at 6:00 or 7:00 PM, they gathered 40 or 50 hooligans to cause trouble, making a scene. Fortunately, no major incident occurred.

Negotiations with the Police Station

Unexpectedly, yesterday at noon, three strange men suddenly came. Two of them held handguns, and one held a box cannon. They broke into the agency and handcuffed Gu Xiujin and Ni Adi, both male and female, forcing them into a car and sped off towards western Shanghai. Afterwards, it was learned that the car with license plate number 17906 belonged to the Xiangxing Automobile Company. The driver, named Yin Guoliang, was a local, 34 years old, and his driver number was 340. He has already reported the incident to the Laozha Police Station. He said that at approximately 12:10 PM, three customers came to the Xiangsheng Company branch near Zhaofeng Garden at the end of Yuyuan Road. The accountant ordered him to drive. When they reached the entrance of Jingqingfang on Guangxi Road, he was instructed to stop the car. The three men then walked into the alley. Before long, a man and a woman were escorted into the car and forced him to drive to western Shanghai. They are now being held at a certain location on 　　Road. The police have been notified and have ordered a Japanese police officer to go and negotiate and demand extradition. It is said that the other party has not yet agreed.

Bloodshed at the Cosmopolitan Dance Hall - Xie Ziting Shot Dead - Shot and Killed Leaving the Dance Hall and Entering a Car at 11:00 PM Last Night

An assassination occurred at the entrance of the Cosmopolitan Garden Dance Hall on Gordon Road at approximately 10:55 PM last night. The victim was Xie Ziting, a local, over 50 years old. He was shot four times and died instantly. The perpetrators were two men who escaped without a trace. Details of the situation have been learned and are provided below.

Brief History of the Deceased

Xie Ziting, a local, whose style name was Qingmo, was formerly the manager of the Zhongfu Bank. He used to reside in Gouyu Lane in Xiaonanmen, Nanshi, and had a good reputation. Later, he moved to Fan Garden on Haig Road. He once held an important position in the former municipal government and currently works for the fake consolidated tax bureau. He moved to a certain residence on Dunxin Road on Great Western Road. At approximately 10:00 PM last night, Xie took a black-plated car with license plate number 9107 to the Cosmopolitan Dance Hall on Gordon Road and danced with the dance hall's star, Chen Mingming.

Murdered After Dancing

At approximately 10:55 PM, when the dancing became less lively, he walked out of the establishment and hired a silver car (license plate number 18270) to return to his residence. When the car arrived in front of the gate, just as he was stepping into the car, unexpectedly, two perpetrators suddenly emerged from Maibian Road nearby, one wearing a Paisley suit and the other a black long gown, and rushed to the side of the car. The man in the suit forcibly dragged Xie out of the car, turned his body around, and fired four shots in a row, all of which hit their mark: one shot in the right arm, one in the left armpit, one in the back, and one in the back of the neck. Xie fell to the ground in response and died on the spot. The murderers, seeing that their goal had been achieved, fled without a trace. Afterwards, the dance hall reported the incident to the Jing'an Temple Police Station, which sent Chinese and Western detectives to investigate and transported the body to Baolong Hospital. The police station is currently investigating the cause of the shooting.

Eccentric Personality

When the reporter rushed to the scene of the incident to investigate, he saw bloodstains all over the entrance, which was chilling. It is reported that Xie went to the dance hall to dance every night at 9:00 or 10:00 PM and had an inextricable bond with the dance hall star Chen Mingming, which has lasted for more than four months. Every day, he signed a "bill," the English writing of which was "C.D.H.ia." At the end of the month, he would go to the dance hall's accounting room to settle the accounts himself. Chen Mingming later told people that Xie came here every night, and when asked about his family history, he looked sad and unhappy, and changed the subject. Moreover, he had an eccentric personality and was taciturn. General speculation is that his sudden shooting may be related to politics. When Xie was killed, he was wearing a light blue striped suit, a black silk handkerchief with white flowers, and yellow leather shoes. His hair was combed back, and he looked like a dignified upper-class figure. Although he was over 50 years old, he looked like a middle-aged man.

Father-in-Law Accuses Son-in-Law of Embezzling Wood Planks - Defendant Released on Bail and Rearrested

Hong Xinghua, the owner of Hong Shenji Timber Company at No. 　, Anrenli, Shanhai Pass Road, is a local, 25 years old. Several years ago, through a matchmaker, he married the daughter of Zhang Jusheng, the manager of Yongtai Shenji Timber Company at No. 208, Luban Road, French Concession, who is from Wuxing. Recently, Zhang Jusheng suddenly hired lawyer Qian and accused his son-in-law Hong Xinghua to the Xinzha Police Station of embezzling fir planks worth 15,000 yuan. Yesterday, Chinese detective Sun Guihua and Western detective Litt arrested Hong and took him to the police station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Second Criminal Division of the First Special Court. Police station lawyer Zhang Tianyin briefly described the case, saying that the plaintiff and defendant were related as father-in-law and son-in-law. In February of this year, the plaintiff entrusted the defendant to handle 400 pieces of pine planks and 500 pieces of fir planks in Fuzhou, totaling 8,200 yuan. The money has been paid and receipts are held. Later, the plaintiff only received 400 pieces of pine planks, and the remaining 500 pieces of fir planks, worth 15,000 yuan at the current market price, were not received. The plaintiff later found out that the fir planks had been transported to Shanghai and pledged by the defendant to Ye Chuansheng. This batch of goods is still in the customs broker's office. Therefore, he is prosecuting based on Article 336, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Law. When questioned, the defendant hired lawyers Wang Yaoting and Wu Zhiping to appear in court, arguing that the case was entirely a civil matter and that the plaintiff was acting out of spite to make the defendant subject to criminal punishment because the defendant had recently had a dispute with his wife in order to protect her mother. In March of this year, the defendant was entrusted by the plaintiff to handle one-inch and four-and-a-half-inch pine planks and box planks, and received 16,000 ocean dollars in Shanghai and another 7,000 yuan in Fuzhou. The goods have been prepared and are being loaded. Unexpectedly, because of a dispute between the defendant and his wife, the plaintiff automatically instructed Fuzhou to stop loading the goods and reported it to the police station. The goods that have arrived in Shanghai are another batch of seven-point fir planks, which were ordered by Yichengchang Timber Company. Now, Yichengchang Timber Company has also hired lawyer Zhao Chuanding to appear in court, which can prove this. Furthermore, the defendant was arrested once on April 30. At that time, the plaintiff forced the defendant to write a note. The defendant had no way to resist and had to obey. However, after being released, the defendant, out of anger, entrusted lawyer Wu Zhiping to publish a statement in the newspaper denying the validity of the note, stating that the two notes were not from the defendant's true intentions. As a result, the plaintiff reported the case to the police station again, and the defendant was detained for the second time. Now, he is requesting permission to post bail. The judge announced that the evidence submitted by the plaintiff was mostly inconsistent. The defendant was ordered to post bail of 15,000 yuan, and the hearing was rescheduled for the 15th.

The exchange rate for British pounds was changed to three pence and one-eighth, and the exchange rate for U.S. dollars was changed to four and a half yuan. As for the domestic market situation, it was neither tight nor loose, and seemed to be entering a stable state. This was because the Hong Kong Telegraph's opening prices of three pence and fifteen sixty-two five per shilling and four yuan and fifty-six sixty-two five per U.S. dollar were maintained as much as possible, making it difficult for speculators to use their skills. Many of them sold into the market, causing the market to become quite rigid for a time. At one point, the hardest British pound was three pence and three seventy-five, and the U.S. dollar reached four yuan and eight seventy-five. However, because the Bank of England, HSBC, and stomach were very good, Chinese merchants and speculators also turned to plugging, causing a softening to appear. The afternoon was even stronger. In the early afternoon, the softening continued to the maintained supply price of Hong Kong. Speculators suddenly changed from plugging back to digging, and the foreign banks' limited appetite and heavy weighting reappeared, turning loose again. In the end, the spot and forward prices of British and American currencies tended to loosen, spot prices were particularly hard, and the swap spread opened up even more. It was heard that at noon, Chinese banks and a certain American bank were willing to sell spot and swap May contracts, posting a U.S. dollar spread of three corners and seventy-five points, with the interest rate reaching more than eight points. However, because cash was exhausted, it was difficult for arbitrageurs to be active.

The Situation Already Shows Loosening

At the beginning of the morning, the exchange rates of British pounds against U.S. dollars, Shanghai dollars, and French francs were all flat. The U.S. dollar fell three seventy-five against the British pound, five points against the Shanghai dollar, and half a point against the French franc. The central listed exchange rates remained the same. HSBC's listed prices were announced, and they were all slightly longer. First Press, Then Lift: Extreme Anxiety in the Gold Market; Peak Reaches 7250 Yuan, Fluctuating 540 Yuan

Yesterday, the cash gold market was volatile, rising more than it fell, but people were uneasy and lacked firm buying and selling intentions. Therefore, it was expected that prices above 7,000 yuan might experience some consolidation. In the early morning, due to the sudden easing of the exchange rate, the price dropped from the opening of 6,800 yuan to 6,710 yuan. Gold shops were reportedly selling, but as the foreign exchange rate softened, the trend reversed. Banks and gold shops successively bought in, and by noon, the price had reached 6,970 yuan. Although a gold shop pushed down the price at the close of the morning session, news of favorable rumors concerning the European war spread, and gold shops aggressively raised prices, exceeding 7,000 yuan to reach 7,030 yuan. Later, as the foreign exchange market reported tighter conditions, the opening price was 7,100 yuan, and soon a new unprecedented peak of 7,250 yuan was reached. One gold shop took the lead in aggressively raising prices, but later a securities firm and another gold shop began selling, and the exchange rate slightly recovered, causing the price to gradually fall back to the 7,000 yuan level. The closing price was 7,010 yuan, 100 yuan higher than the previous weekend. The total trading volume for the day was over 4,000 taels. Silver jewelry prices fluctuated, ultimately increasing by 20 yuan. Customs gold prices remained unchanged.

Gold Bullion Still Up 100 Yuan

Since the morning, each tael (ten taels) initially reported a loose exchange market, and people's hearts were slightly frustrated. The market opened 110 yuan lower, with gold shops selling 20 taels to banks at 6,800 yuan. Subsequently, due to strong selling by gold shops, the price fell again by 90 yuan, reaching a low of 6,710 yuan. However, the trading volume was very small. The banks' buying gradually strengthened, and the market turned upward. Soon, the price returned to the 6,800 yuan level. Later, the foreign exchange market suddenly reported softening, boosting morale further, and securities firms rushed to buy, raising the price by several tens of yuan. Banks traded with each other at 6,900 yuan per tael. Afterwards, as speculators took the opportunity to sell, and buyers gradually decreased, the price fell back by 100 yuan. Speculators sold 30 taels to banks at 6,800 yuan. However, gold shops later bought in, and banks also competed to buy, and as the foreign exchange market continued to report tightening, the price jumped by 170 yuan. Gold shops bought several tens of taels from gold shops and banks, all at 6,970 yuan. Near the close, a gold shop disregarded the market price and pushed the price down by selling, closing at 6,965 yuan. After the close, another gold shop aggressively raised prices, reportedly due to favorable news from Europe, causing sellers to hesitate and raising the price to 7,030 yuan. The trading volume was extremely small. In the afternoon, the foreign exchange market reported tighter conditions, boosting morale further. The opening price jumped to 7,100 yuan, and then, with gold shops and retail investors rushing to buy, the price soared again by 150 yuan. Gold shops bought 30 taels from banks at an unprecedented high price of 7,250 yuan. Shortly after, the number of buyers decreased, and selling pressure intensified, gradually falling back to 7,200 yuan. The market became quiet for a time, with slight consolidation. Later, as the foreign exchange market hardened, selling increased, and gold shops and securities firms competed to sell, soon dropping by nearly 200 yuan. Gold shops sold 20 taels to securities firms at 7,000 yuan. At that time, speculators and scalpers frequently bought in, pushing the price up to 7,080 yuan. However, eventually, due to further selling by gold shops, and retail investors stopping buying, the price fell back by nearly 70 yuan. Securities firms sold 20 taels to gold shops, closing at 7,010 yuan. As a result, the price was 100 yuan higher than the previous Saturday, with a total fluctuation of 540 yuan throughout the day.
