Securities: Active Foreign Shares, Increased Trading

Yesterday's securities market was characterized by the fact that although the bulls were struggling, they were still unable to raise their heads. Rumors were rampant, changing rapidly, and people's hearts were shaken and restless. Cautious people mostly held back, and those forced by financial constraints mostly sold. There were few short covering, and even fewer bulls. The monthly interest rate on loans was as high as 40 to 50 percent, so the market price of government bonds was weak, and trading decreased significantly. In the morning, more Tungsun shares were sold, and more Lianhe and Tiansheng shares were also sold. Changji and Tung Yu bought slightly. In the afternoon, more Tungsih shares were sold, and Lianhe also continued to sell. Xinfu and Hongda bulls settled slightly, and Yuankang, Suifu, and retail investors bought. The market still turned from high to low. The result was mixed, with a difference of only 5 cents to 2.5 cents per share. The trading volume was only around 500,000 yuan. A simple table is listed below.

200 shares of Hanyeping shares were traded at a price of 4.25 yuan. The Shanghai Chinese General Chamber of Commerce stock market opened vigorously, and trading increased gradually. The price was much higher than the closing price on the previous Friday. There were no major disturbances that day, and the trend was firm, with no sign of turning back for a while.

British & Foreign shares once again occupied the top spot among industrial shares. 52,100 shares were traded, and the price also increased the most compared to the previous week's close. It once reached 75 yuan, and the closing price was 73 yuan with buyers. The other popular shares were International and Jardine Matheson, etc.

The trading volume of Yeguang shares was large, but the price change was very small. After seeing a high price of 17.4 yuan, it returned to 17.2 yuan at the close. The shares that were sold were the easiest to absorb.

From yesterday onwards, all prices of Wheelock Marden shares were marked with the words "ex-rights." The "new share rights" were traded separately. This complicated relationship initially caused hesitation among the general public, resulting in a long delay in trading. Operators needed to think carefully to determine the connection value between the two, so that they could compare them with the closing price of "speed rights" shares from the previous week. After a while, ex-rights shares were traded at 130 yuan, and new share rights were traded at 100 yuan. At the close, the former was 131 yuan and the latter was 98 yuan. Purchasers of new share rights had to pay 25 yuan per share to the company, so the total capital of each new share was 123 yuan. However, the interest on this new share would be calculated from April 1st onwards, and the company's operating profit before that would not be included. Although the exact amount of the old share is unknown, it is believed that there is still a final dividend to be paid. Purchasers should not ignore this, and the difference between the two share prices can be regarded as the market's imagined final dividend of the old share.

Rubber shares were in great demand, and the trend of each share was very active. However, the prices of each share did not rise in the same proportion. The following several types were particularly obvious.

British & Foreign Java closed at 56 yuan the previous day and 60 yuan yesterday. British & Foreign Kotah closed at 29 yuan the previous day and 31.5 yuan yesterday. Langkat closed at 39 yuan the previous day and 47 yuan yesterday. Rubber Trust closed at 37.25 yuan the previous day and 39.25 yuan yesterday. All the above rubber companies are located in the Dutch East Indies, so the only reason they are popular is undoubtedly that these companies are not subject to the foreign exchange restriction regulations, unlike many other British Malayan companies.

Grains: Exchange Rate Slightly Eases, Foreign Rice Dumped, Demand Surges

The rice market, due to the unexpected surge in gold prices, initially seemed difficult to contain. However, the market is volatile, and as the gold market and exchange rate stabilized, a downward trend was seen. The initial opening in the morning saw limited activity, and the market was relatively stable. Then, news spread of falling gold prices and a looser exchange rate, causing changes to occur. Calls for sales spread throughout the market, with tight capital and everyone rushing to dump their holdings, resulting in chaos and a loss of market benchmarks. Price declines were inconsistent. Siaochiao rose three levels, while Saigon depreciated nine yards. This is because Siaochiao has recently been entirely controlled by speculation and is most active. Although there are fluctuations, it is mainly a rise with small declines. Yesterday, the lowest price was still 48.8 yuan, and by the close, it still reached 49.5 yuan, only depreciating by half a yuan compared to the previous week's closing price of 50 yuan. The situation for other goods was completely different, with actual sales being slow and fathers being neglected by the mind, leading to a small movement of inventory, deviating from the norm, and falling by two or three yuan. In the past, Niangti rice was priced three or four yuan, or one or two yuan higher than Siaochiao, but now its sales price is almost equal to Siaochiao. The closing price for Saigon No. 1 was only 50 yuan, Saigon No. 2 was around 49 yuan, Siam and fire milled rice were 49.5 yuan, and Siam No. 2 was even cheaper, shorter than Siaochiao by more than one yuan, opening at only 48.3-48.4 yuan. This kind of abnormal development is truly the result of the speculation transaction, which has been rarely seen in the past. Fortunately, the market for broken rice and rice bran was not large, so it was able to maintain its own identity without much fluctuation. High quality rice still sold for 45.5 to 45 yuan, and special broken rice ranged from 43.2 to 40 yuan.

The source of japonica rice from the mainland has become increasingly scarce due to transportation issues. Although the demand from the sales market seems to be strong, it is also constrained by foreign rice and is falling by about one yuan. Special grade Wuxi japonica rice is 51-52 yuan, powdered japonica rice is 50 yuan, Changkun japonica rice is 51-50 yuan, Zhongsu japonica rice is 47-48 yuan, and Qing Si special grade thin rice is 50-48.5 yuan. Nangang early rice rose from 49.5 yuan to 48 yuan.

Glutinous rice was originally slow to move, but it is now even more weak and lacking in spirit. Therefore, Jinli rice, originally 43.5-43 yuan, has been lowered to 41-42 yuan, while the worst quality sold for 39.5 yuan, which is more than one yuan lower than the previous trading session.

Yesterday, the foreign rice market had leveled off, as the previous days' soaring prices were entirely created by speculators. In reality, official transactions were observing. Yesterday's market transactions were still driven by speculation, so the market price rose and fell rapidly, changing in an instant. However, with the exchange rate loosening, the price of rice slightly recovered a few cents. Currently, Siaochiao rice is the most popular, with fluctuating prices. The opening price in the morning was 50.3 yuan, rising to 50.5 yuan, and then immediately falling to 48.7 yuan. After rising once in the afternoon, the final price was 49.4 yuan, with no buyers. The prices of other types of rice all showed fluctuations. The returned Saigon No. 2 opened at 59 yuan and closed at 59.7 yuan in the afternoon. The weakness of Xing rice has reached 58.35-58.4 yuan per original package with small grain. The total volume of spot rice traded was 8-9 thousand bags, and the returned original packages totaled more than 600 tons.

Also, foreign rice arrived in Shanghai yesterday, totaling 5,172 bags, shipped from Hong Kong by Jardine Matheson's Yüsheng vessel.

Flour Market Firm, -- Wheat Still Holding Strong --

The Shunfeng brand produced by the Wuxi mill opened at 14.3 yuan, and later 2-3 thousand bags were traded at 14.25-14.2 yuan. The market is gradually becoming firm.

The buying and selling of wheat yesterday was still holding strong, and the market had not much change.

Educational News

Tumultuous Controversy in the American Education Community: Dr. Russell Ruled by the Court Not to Teach at New York College

The renowned British philosopher and mathematician Dr. Russell, formerly a British Earl, abandoned his noble status, preferring to live as a commoner. He is currently a philosophy professor at the University of California. On February 26th of this year, the City College of New York hired him to be a philosophy professor from February next year, with an annual remuneration of $8,000. A Mrs. Kai, whose two children have reached school age, petitioned the New York City Board of Higher Education on March 19th in her capacity as a taxpayer. She argued that Russell advocated "immoral and obscene free love doctrines" as a reason to terminate his employment. On March 30th, Justice McCook of the New York State Supreme Court ruled that hiring Russell as a professor at the City College was not only "a stain on academic integrity" but also "an insult to the residents of New York City," and ordered the City Board of Higher Education to terminate Russell's employment.

The judgment document is seventeen pages long and states that according to the New York State Education Law, Russell, not having obtained American citizenship, cannot teach in the state. The New York City Board of Higher Education's approval of Russell's employment without examination procedures also violated the New York State Constitution. "Most unconscionable" was that such employment would "endanger the public health, safety, and morals of the people."

After the verdict was announced, Mrs. Kai called it "a victory for every parent in New York City and a victory for justice and purity." Professor Russell, from the University of California in Los Angeles, cabled that "he did not want to comment at this stage and was seeking legal advice." It is also unknown whether the Board of Higher Education will appeal. The American Civil Liberties Union has cabled Russell, expressing its willingness to provide support. Bishop Manning, who first attacked Russell in an open letter to the newspaper on March 1st, "does not want to comment at this time."

Dr. Hotchkiss, Vice President of the University of California, said that the school had no criticism of Russell's scholarship and teaching methods. His decision to leave the school this spring was entirely voluntary. Payne, editor of the California student publication, expressed his opinion, saying, "This matter is a tragedy for American education. The New York State Court's ruling that Russell is not qualified to teach in the state is nonsensical. No professor I have studied with surpasses Russell. His students must be outraged by this verdict. If the University of California can find a way to retain Russell, the entire faculty and student body would welcome it. I took two courses taught by Russell and never heard him mention any moral issues."

Russell's third wife, Patricia, said, "We are guests in a foreign land and do not know the legal procedures. How to proceed will be handled by lawyers in New York. Although we do not want to cause trouble, we have no choice. The crux of this case is an issue of civil rights and academic freedom, concerning countless intellectuals. We cannot remain silent at this point." Russell's students are petitioning the University of California authorities to retain him, and many of his colleagues have also risen to defend him. Dr. Reichenbach, a philosophy professor at California, said, "We all know that Professor Russell is a great philosopher of our time. This verdict by the New York court is outrageous." Russell's student, Betty, said, "It is a rare privilege to hear Dr. Russell lecture. He is indeed a noble scholar, and my morals have never been corrupted by him."

When Justice McCook distributed the judgment to reporters, he said that he had studied Russell's works late into the night before making this judgment. The first six pages of the judgment explained the issues of citizenship and examination, while the remaining eleven pages denounced Russell's views on sexual behavior, citing the theories in four of Russell's books as the basis. The judgment concluded, "Teachers have more power to influence students' thoughts than various terms. Assuming Russell were allowed to teach at the City College for two years without promoting his views, it would still violate the academic regulations mentioned above. Russell's philosophy and behavior directly contradict New York State criminal law. Academic freedom, a right, should never be used as a pretext to mislead young people and violate criminal law." (Translated from the March 31st New York Herald Tribune)

Schools Also Offer Social Education

The Ministry of Education Formulates Promotion Measures

(Chongqing, 6th) In order to promote social education through schools, the Ministry of Education has formulated six promotion measures and issued them to all provinces and cities for compliance. In the future, provincial, municipal, and county budgets should add appropriations for subsidizing schools to offer social education in accordance with regulations.

Reorganization and Establishment of the Board of Directors of the Chinese Medical College

The Board of Directors of the Chinese Medical College on Chongqing Road, Shanghai, has been reorganized following the resignation of Presidents Qin and Ma. The first meeting was held on the 3rd, with directors Lin Kanghou, Wen Lanting, Xu Xiaochu, Yang Yusheng, and Zhu Hegao attending. Lin Kanghou was elected as Chairman of the Board, Zhu Hegao was appointed as President, and Qin Bowei was appointed as Honorary President. Classes will resume on the 6th. The college's charter has been revised and submitted to the ministry for approval.

Harvard University Declares Russell's Appointment Still Valid

The New York Times reported that Harvard University officials stated that the university had already hired Professor Russell as a lecturer in philosophy and semantic evolution for half a semester. Although the New York Supreme Court has ruled that Russell is not allowed to teach at the City College of New York, Harvard University's appointment is not affected. The university has always advocated that all teachers should enjoy "academic freedom." According to reports, when Harvard University announced the appointment of Russell as a lecturer two years ago, Massachusetts State Representative Dooling also protested, citing the same reasons as those listed in New York. Before the New York City Board of Higher Education's decision, there was a great dispute in the church and education communities regarding the issue of hiring Russell. Therefore, a special meeting was held to discuss it, and by a vote of eleven to seven, the motion to reconsider Russell's employment was defeated. Russell is 67 years old and has been divorced twice. He is now married for the third time.

Old News Re-Copied: Sixty-Seven Years Ago (1937)

Spring Welcoming Ceremony

Although welcoming spring is an ancient custom, the ceremonial arrangements are the same everywhere. This year's spring welcoming ceremony in Hangzhou is more elaborate than in previous years, also a sign of peace and prosperity. On the 13th day of the first month, the weather was clear and fine. Spectators filled the area from Qingchun Gate to the intersection of Puan Street, as well as Henghe Bridge and Shipailou, a distance of three or four li, with hardly any space to stand. On that day, the three prefectural officials and the officials of the two counties under its jurisdiction, all dressed in their official robes and hats, arranged a full set of ceremonial items. They went to the Governor's office to offer spring greetings, then took warm sedan chairs out of Qingchun Gate to Shangxin Temple. First, they performed the spring plowing ceremony, then respectfully welcomed the God of Spring into the city. The officials then changed to ornate sedan chairs and returned to their offices. The God of Spring was then paraded around to the various government offices. The next day, he was taken to the Wushan Tai Sui Temple to be enshrined, restoring him to his former position. When welcoming the spring, around noon, the sound of gongs and drums vibrated, and the sound of Sheng and Guan harmonized. First, there were several decorated pavilions, each with vases and other items. Next, there were dozens of pairs of gold-lettered plaques, all with phrases such as "Good weather for the crops," "Five grains abundant," and so on. Then there were four raised platforms, each with two people dressed as the Eight Immortals. Following them was a paper ox, carried on poles, with the same colors as depicted in the Spring Ox Diagram. Behind it was a person leading a live ox slowly, as it was the ox that the Tai Sui would plow with. People seeing it would scramble to pull out its hair, believing it would bring good luck. In the afternoon, there was usually a spring official, who often mingled in the crowd, making it impossible to identify him. This was because the people of Hangzhou would scramble to beat the spring official, calling it "Beating the Spring." The ceremony will be continued tomorrow.

Free Talk

Being a World Citizen (3)

What should we do? Science is valuable and must be preserved. So, let's eliminate narrow-mindedness. But how do we eliminate it? Honestly, we all have this narrow-minded tendency. We are narrow, selfish, and cruel, but to varying degrees. Are we going to eliminate humanity to eradicate it? That won't work. We have to settle for the next best thing: transforming narrow-minded people into broad-minded people, short people into giants, and narrow-minded people into godly beings. Therefore, people today need the following three things: (1) A world-mindedness: A person's mind should be broad, not just deep. Narrow-minded people have narrow minds, while godly people have broad minds. If you want to know how broad-minded someone is, just look at what they pray for. For example, if someone only prays four times for us and then stops, you know how narrow-minded they are. Most people pray like this: "God, watch over my child at school, Jane in the office, Mom in the kitchen, and Dad in the factory, Amen." But don't they know that there are more people than just these who need our prayers? That's why Jesus taught us to pray, "Our Father," "Our daily bread," "Our sins." The word "our" includes everyone. A new magazine in the United States called "World Affairs" discusses all issues from a global perspective. If we read this magazine, our minds will become world-minded. When we pray, we won't limit ourselves to our own families. We'll include black, white, red, yellow, and people of all colors in our prayers. This is one of the greatest needs. (2) A world-conscience: Everyone has a conscience. However, some people have narrow consciences. They have a conscience in certain places or about certain things, but not in others. For example, someone may not want to steal from their mother, but they will take the opportunity to rob their neighbors. Such a conscience is a threat to social security. (To be continued) For detailed study, please write to P.O. Box 1227.

Science

On the Physique of the Chinese Nation from an Anthropological Perspective

— Nan Jun

In this day of bloody strife, the law of the jungle seems to have become the common rule of evolution. The fact that our great Chinese nation is being trampled upon by others is undeniable. The external pressure and urgency of national subjugation and racial extinction are recognized by everyone as having reached the most critical point. We must grit our teeth, exert our greatest strength in resistance, and embark on a bright path to seek human freedom and equality. However, some patriots often think of the question of racial inferiority, that is, "What are the strengths and weaknesses of the Chinese nation?" Indeed, the rise and fall of a nation and the prosperity and decline of a race involve various complex factors. But from the perspective of the nation itself, it occupies an important position among these factors. We will temporarily set aside the facts of spiritual culture and, from an anthropological viewpoint, analyze the physique of the nation to understand our own physical condition in the world. This is also a meaningful thing.

Based on known materials, the physique of the Chinese nation can be analyzed according to the criteria of human classification to obtain the following results. These contributions from anthropologists are indeed common knowledge that ordinary people should know to understand themselves. For the sake of clarity, they are described as follows:

Height: The height of Chinese people varies from north to south. The average height of people in Hebei is 1690 mm, while the average height of people in Guangdong is 1618 mm, a difference of 72 mm. The other provinces are in between these two extremes. From this, it can be seen that the height of Chinese people can be classified into three categories: tallest, tall, and medium. At the same time, it can be said that the height of Chinese people is directly proportional to geographical latitude. Compared with the world's population, we are in the "medium" category.

Head Shape: Head shape is the most important standard for human classification, generally divided into three types, according to the cephalic index. Long-headed people account for 14.41% of Chinese people, medium-headed people account for 42.14%, and broad-headed people account for 43.47%. In terms of geographical distribution, long-headed people are more common in the north, called the Yellow River type; medium-headed people are more common in the central region, called the Yangtze River type; and broad-headed people are more common in the south, called the Pearl River type. The size of the head shape is closely related to brain capacity. From an evolutionary perspective, the degree of evolution of broad-headed and medium-headed people is higher.

Hair: The hair of Chinese people is a coarse, long, straight hair, rarely curly or wavy. The cross-section under a microscope is round or nearly round, and usually black. According to anatomical studies, wavy hair is closest to apes, followed by straight hair, and woolly hair is the highest. From the perspective of human evolutionary history, because our body hair is sparse, we seem to be far above Caucasians. Furthermore, according to the law of heredity, black hair is superior in color. Therefore, our hair is indeed in the highest position in the evolution of the world's population.

Skin Color: The superiority of skin color in the evolutionary process does not involve aesthetic considerations. From the facts of disease resistance, it is known that black skin is the strongest, followed by yellow skin, and white skin is the weakest. Yellow people are easily adaptable to both cold and hot zones, so Chinese people can live no matter where they emigrate, and rarely suffer from illness due to acclimatization. This advantage is a natural characteristic of yellow skin.

Lips: The thickness of the lips is also an important piece of evidence in human evolution. According to animal morphology, the lips of Caucasians are the thinnest, which seems to be closer to apes, followed by yellow people, and black people are indeed the most "humanized".

Facial Angle: A straight line from the forehead to the tip of the nose, and another line from the nose to the ear, the angle formed by the intersection of the two lines is called the facial angle. According to the inference of evolutionary theory, the greater the facial verticality, that is, the smaller the facial angle, the lower his intelligence; conversely, it is higher. The facial angle of Chinese people is between that of black and white people. If intelligence is indeed closely related to the size of the facial angle, then their natural intelligence belongs to the middle level, not inferior.

Eyes: The eye color of Chinese people is usually dark brown, not black. The degree of opening is medium, and there is often a layer called the "Mongolian fold" at the inner corner near the nose, but its function is unknown. The shape of the eyes is slightly slanted, called almond eyes, that is, the outer corner is slightly higher than the inner corner.

Nose: In the evolutionary process, the nose shape of Caucasians is high and narrow, occupying the most superior position. Most Chinese people have medium noses, and the form of broad noses is especially prominent in southern people, perhaps due to climate reasons. In this respect, Chinese people seem to be lower.

The above-mentioned points are the criteria used in racial taxonomy. Upon close examination, it is known that the physical structure of Chinese people is not in an inferior position. Compared with other races in the world, it shows many advantages, and shows the fact of "medium" everywhere. Thinking from the standpoint of biological evolution, "medium" may be the result of eliminating inferiority and retaining superiority. With this kind of scientific analysis, it can greatly break our self-doubting concepts. From this, it can be seen that today's being invaded by others is definitely not based on the problem of racial inferiority. Of course, there are other complex factors, such as social organization, political system, popular knowledge, and patriotic thought, which are very important factors.

We don't need to despise each other, and we should unite the entire nation as one. "Know yourself first, and then proceed with your work" is a commendable motto. Indeed, ancient nations inevitably decline, but new stimuli, pressures, and trampling may also be the greatest driving force for regeneration. A glorious future will be opened up from this.

Anecdotes

The Entertainment of Heads of State

— Song Jinglian

According to recent news from Cairo, the capital of Egypt, the eighteen-year-old King Farouk of Egypt is preparing to take a pilot test in order to obtain a pilot's license. In fact, this news is not surprising to those who know the king, because King Farouk is exceptionally healthy and is already very fond of various outdoor sports.

Since the tragedies of King Albert of Belgium falling to his death while mountaineering in 1934 and the Queen of Belgium dying in a car accident in 1935, heads of state around the world still take dangerous sports (such as flying and driving) as their leisure activities, just as King Farouk of Egypt is dedicated to driving airplanes.

However, the life of a head of state is very important, so the British House of Commons has intervened in this matter. The House of Commons requested King George V to order the then heir to the throne, the Prince of Wales (later Edward VIII, now the Duke of Windsor), not to ride horses excessively. George V himself was also very fond of horseback riding. He would ride a horse to Hyde Park every day and was also good at yachting and a skilled helmsman. The boldest was former King Alfonso XIII of Spain. He was a good horse rider and car driver. When he was traveling in Bordeaux, France, he was stopped by a traffic police officer for speeding.

King Carol of Romania now only plays with his son by riding horses and skating. Before he ascended the throne, he loved flying and took an airplane to regain the throne.

King Boris of Bulgaria likes to drive cars and trucks at high speed on the rugged roads of Bulgaria. He also likes to drive trains and has obtained a license from Bulgarian railway technicians and is honored to be elected as the honorary president of the Railway Workers' Union.

As for the entertainment of the Emperor of Sweden, I think everyone knows that he is a tennis master.

Prince Olav of Norway likes to ride motorcycles.

The elderly King Christian of Denmark likes to travel by bicycle.

Hitler does not like outdoor sports. As for his brother in difficulty, Mussolini, it is the opposite. Whether it is airplanes, cars, motorcycles, horseback riding, swimming, race walking... he has a share in everything. Mussolini is indeed versatile and can also speak several languages!

French President Lebrun likes to ride horses and stroll in the Rambouillet forest.

The entertainment of the following heads of state is very different from the above, and is in the field of art: King Carlos I of Portugal, who was assassinated in 1908, was a famous painter and won gold medals twice at the French Salon exhibition and the Paris Exposition in 1900.

Queen Mother Elizabeth of Romania, who came from the British royal family, is a prolific writer. In history, Queen Victoria was good at painting, especially depicting rural scenery, and always had a small sketchbook in her luggage. The unparalleled beauty Queen Marie Antoinette liked to carve scenes of Paris on buttons. Napoleon III's mother was good at watercolor painting and portraiture.

Now let's talk about Hitler. Although he is not good at sports, he is a painter. A few years ago, the editor-in-chief of the Berliner Morgenpost published a collection of watercolors, which included the works of a corporal during the European War, signed Adolf Hitler.

Hygiene

Do Not Abuse Your Spirit

— Chen Shichao

I often see many patients who become weak due to overwork, and then catch a cold and are bedridden. Those who are stubborn insist on persevering, but greater hidden damage breaks out, forcing them to fall into bed. The period for seeing a doctor is one week for the former, and even two or three years for the latter. The medical expenses are of course considerable, and the loss of business for a week or two or three years is even greater. The working time in a day is eight hours. When you work for ten hours and think you are diligent enough, you don't know that you have lost a portion of your spirit that must be preserved. After a month or two, you will gradually feel unsustainable. If you continue to do this, you will need to rest for a longer period. Then, your business will stop, your savings will be depleted, and time will slowly pass.

If you have to work so hard because of the heavy burden of life, please pay attention to the following points: go to bed early, sleep more, be silent, worry less, and avoid wild thoughts. As for playing cards, making trouble, and drinking excessive alcohol, these are not games that benefit the body and mind. Normal entertainment, such as music and walking, are free and may be increased appropriately.

Entertainment World

Film Workers' Guide: The Functions and Responsibilities of Cinematography

— De

There are good film criticisms in the newspapers, but there are also bad ones. He would blame the actors for the director's mistakes; he would attribute the director's strengths to the cinematographer. Here I briefly explain the six major functions and responsibilities of film art, hoping that the general audience and film critics will use a more advanced perspective to examine the merits and demerits of a film:

Screenwriter

His responsibility is to make the theme of a movie upright, the content rich, and in line with the times. He must avoid unclear themes, empty content, banality, absurdity, nonsense, no social significance, and no artistic value, etc.

Director

He wants to use film techniques to concretely put the script handed down by the screenwriter on the screen. He has to manage the rhythm of the whole play. Where can he be understated? Where should important arrangements be made? How to grasp the key moment of the play? How to prevent the audience's mood from relaxing? He also has to clearly distinguish the personalities of each character in the play, and do not make an actor suddenly reveal different personalities in the same play. He should mobilize other collaborators, such as musicians, sound engineers, and cinematographers, to help the progress of his play, and how to control his actors from acting like a civilized drama.

Actor

Whether he personally does well, does well. He should carefully study the role he plays. Personality, action, tone, attitude, demeanor, how a certain scene should be expressed, and how a certain scene should reveal his true feelings. If he is underdone or overdone, and his movements and attitudes are not enough of an artist's status, then it is his mistake.

Set Designer

He should arrange to create a "environment" suitable for the plot, and whether the atmosphere of the scene is sufficient is also worth investigating.

Cinematographer

Lighting is his important mission. The light money for each scene should be completely unified. Strong scenes should use hard lines and lighting. Beautiful and lyrical scenes should use soft and light tones. Happy scenes should use bright tones, and so on.

Sound Engineer

His responsibility is to adjust the language and sound. The pitch and intensity of the sound should be suitable for the development of the plot. However, the crudeness of the machinery and other insufficient material conditions are not his fault.

The reporter of this newspaper said the following words at the end of his communication: "The citizens of Chongqing and several other larger cities in inland China, such as Chengdu, are the same. They now crave high-end music as much as other living conditions, so they are very welcome to singing groups from various places to come and perform."

"Su Xijiao" and Zhang Wenyuan's Expression

After Watching Selling Unicorn (Part 2)

— Wei Wo

Because in that play, the faces of "poverty and wealth", "snobbery", "good and evil", "cause and effect", "natural disasters" and "man-made disasters" are thoroughly revealed. Especially the fact that the rich man with ten thousand guans of wealth may immediately become a poor man, as well as the two points of doing good and getting blessings and knowing how to repay kindness, can be said to contain sufficient stimulation in today's world.

The playwright has put a lot of thought into the arrangement, and many humorous dialogues are really to the point, making people laugh and cry. In this satisfactory arrangement, there are many new contributions. Several scenes completely borrow car dialogues and are absolutely dramatized. For example, when there is a flood, the water god is not used to pass the scene, but the crowd shouts "The flood is coming" behind the curtain, which is also a reform worthy of praise. The several plays recently written by Yanqiu do have small reforms that make people's ears and eyes refreshed, and this play is even more progressive.

Speaking of technology, Yanqiu's work has always been admired, especially in acting sad plays. Xue Xiangling in the first part is a daughter of a thousand gold, and Yanqiu still has an extraordinary performance, depicting Xiangling's pampered and extravagant beauty, with graceful and dignified manners. When watching the dowry, the water sleeves have two wonderful postures. Speaking of singing, this play can be said to let the audience enjoy the drama to the fullest. The most important are two segments of erliu, one segment of erhuang, and one segment of xipi. The first segment of erliu is the scene of sheltering from the rain in the Spring and Autumn Pavilion. After this segment of erliu, it turns into a allegro. There is a good tune in the fourth sentence of the blank mouth "Presumably it is a newlywed couple crossing the Magpie Bridge", and there is a good tune in the three words "Crossing the Magpie Bridge". It turns to Allegro later, and there are even better tunes, especially the last sentence of each paragraph, and the closing tune is never the same, which is not easy. Among the lyrics, there are sentences with seven characters and sentences with six characters, which are even more novel. When Ban Tianlin travels to Aunt's place, he sings erhuang slow board, and finally sings a large section of erliu with a crying head. There are many new tunes in total, but due to space limitations, it is not convenient to list them one by one. In short, Yanqiu's tune is not easy to learn in the first place, and the tune used in this play makes people feel that "it sounds good to listen to, but it is difficult to learn." As for the supporting roles, the distribution seems to be slightly inappropriate. Furongcao should play Zhao Shuzhen, and Zhang Chunyan should play Lu Han. It is said that this play by Yanqiu is still being rehearsed for the first time, and for the convenience of future performances, Wu Fuqin is assigned to play Zhao Shuzhen, then the role of Meixiang is quite important. Why not assign Cao Ergeng, but assign Liu Binkun. The performance results show that Liu Binkun's Meixiang is the best. Binkun plays an ugly girl, which is rarely seen, and playing Meixiang in this play is just right. In the same scene as Yanqiu, he has the beauty of setting off the most, and Binkun can not make the audience laugh with his big voice and strange strength. He completely wins with his acting skills and small movements, which is worth applauding. Furongcao's Gu Yunsu's play is not much, and there is no room for his talents. Cao Ergeng's ugly girl and Li Xiaolong's Hu Jie are extremely funny. Wu Fuqin's Zhao Shuzhen and Zhang Chunyan's Xue Liang are both competent. Sun Futing, Li Siguan, Cishaoquan are mediocre. There are many actors in this play, and the entire Huangquan troupe is almost completely dispatched. Judging from the performance results, this play is still worth watching.

The Recording of a Choir's Performance in Chongqing

— Xin Fang

In the past month, a newspaper in Boston, USA, published a Chongqing communication. The content described the recent performance of a choir jointly composed of Chinese and Western followers of Jesus in the local area. Now the original text is excerpted and translated as follows:

The leader of the group is a Canadian named Gada Anniu. There are a total of 58 members, including foreign missionaries and students from the five major universities in Chengdu. A total of three performances were given in Chongqing, and the venue was借借國泰大戲院 (illegible characters). The state of crowding was unbelievable at each performance. As for the songs sung, they can be divided into two types; one is simply irrelevant to the War of Resistance, and the other is absolutely capable of influencing the War of Resistance. The former includes famous songs such as "The Night of the Danube", and the latter includes "Resistance Song" "Song of Resisteuce" compiled by Huang Jun, etc. In addition, a Buddhist hymn was also sung; it is really a strange thing in the world for a choir composed of Jesus's followers to sing a Buddhist hymn. The group has identified 7,000 yuan of the performance income to donate to Chinese war orphans.

Speaking of the activities of the group besides the three performances on stage, it was to accept the welcoming parties from various local parties; and broadcast several times. When Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi often arrived in Chongqing, he specially set up a banquet to wash away the dust.

A Shortcut to Beauty

— Printed

Once, the Paramount Pictures company authorities asked a beautiful actress a question: "What method do you think can make one's appearance beautiful?" Among the answers, twelve people said that sufficient sleep is the best method, three people introduced several beauty products: one said to exercise more and eat fewer snacks, one said to drink more boiled water; and another said to bathe more; all can make one's appearance beautiful.

Jin Suqin and Hua Huilin — Will Perform in Hong Kong

— Sea

Since Jin Suqin's performance at the Lee Theatre did not materialize, she has been enjoying a leisurely life there. She is not preparing to return to Shanghai for the time being. Recently, she asked a friend who came to Shanghai from Hong Kong to get the script and head ornaments of "The Hatred of Life and Death" from her younger sister Suwen, as if she is about to be active again.

The reporter recently received a letter from a friend in Hong Kong, saying that Rui Qingrong is said to be forming a troupe there, preparing to have Jin Suqin and Hua Huilin as the backbone, and is in contact with the Lee Theatre and the Taiping Theatre. Regarding this news, Suwen was asked about it, and she also admitted that there was such a thing. In that case, Suqin's getting the script and head ornaments is a preparation for performing, and not just a coincidence.
